sys_gagarin_init = {
    name = "Gagarin"
    class = "sc_k"
	max_instances = 1
	
	flags = { attican_traverse_system armstrong_nebula_system gagarin_system btr_system custom_system }	
	
	planet = {
		name = "Gagarin"
		class = "pc_k_star"
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = 33
		has_ring = no
		flags = { gagarin_star }	
		init_effect = {
			prevent_anomaly = yes
			clear_deposits = yes

			create_ambient_object = {
				type = "nebula_1"
				entity_offset_height = -5
				location = this
			}
			last_created_ambient_object = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 0
					angle = random
				}
			}
		}		
	}

    planet = {
        name = "Junthor"
        class = "pc_chlorine"
        orbit_distance = 65
        orbit_angle = 165
        has_ring = no
		size = 25 
		init_effect = {

			add_deposit = d_aluminum_surface
			add_deposit = d_aluminum_surface
			add_deposit = d_aluminum_surface
			add_deposit = d_nickel_deposits
			add_deposit = d_nickel_deposits
			add_deposit = d_average_mineral_deposits
			add_deposit = d_junthor_ruins
			set_planet_flag = starting_deposit

			# add_anomaly = {
			# 	category = MEC_EG_ANO_JUNTHOR_1021_CAT			###Junthor Anomaly (Ancient Obelisk)
			# }			
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = junthor_codex_untranslated
				days = -1
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bleak_planet
				days = -1
			}

		}	

		flags = { junthor_planet pd_ignore }		

		moon = {
			name = "Junthor a"
			class = "pc_iron"
			orbit_distance = 9
			size = 5
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
			}						
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Junthor b"
			class = "pc_subglacial"
			orbit_distance = 3
			size = 3	
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				add_deposit = d_average_iridium_deposits
				add_deposit = d_average_palladium_deposits
			}				
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Junthor c"
			class = "pc_barren"
			orbit_distance = 3
			size = 3
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				add_deposit = d_rich_platinum_deposits
			}			
		}		
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Pressha"
        class = "pc_ice_giant"
        orbit_distance = 45
        orbit_angle = 202
        has_ring = no
		size = 30

		flags = { pressha_planet pd_ignore }

			prevent_anomaly = yes

				prevent_anomaly = yes

			}			
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Pressha b"
			class = "pc_frozen"

				prevent_anomaly = yes
				add_deposit = d_poor_palladium_deposits

			}
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Pressha c"
			count = 1
			class = "pc_barren_cold"
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 4
			size = 9
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				add_deposit = d_poor_iridium_deposits
			}
		}		
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Rayingri"
        class = "pc_mephitic"

        has_ring = no
		size = 13

			add_deposit = d_average_palladium_deposits

				days = -1

			}
		}

			class = "pc_iron"
			orbit_distance = 5

				add_modifier = {
					modifier = vahtz_unsurveyed_codex
					days = -1
				}	
				# add_anomaly = {
				# 	category = MEC_EG_ANO_RAYINGRI_1022_CAT			###Rayingri Anomaly (Collision Course)
				# }
			}				
		}
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Sogelrus"
        class = "pc_cryovolcanic"
        orbit_distance = 50
        orbit_angle = 286
        has_ring = no
		size = 11

		flags = { sogelrus_planet pd_ignore }

		init_effect = {

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = sogelrus_codex
			}
		}
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Antirumgon"
        class = "pc_hydrocarbon"
        orbit_distance = 35
        orbit_angle = 289
        has_ring = no
		size = 23

		flags = { antirumgon_planet pd_ignore }	

		init_effect = {
			
			add_deposit = d_poor_mineral_deposits
			add_deposit = d_trade_value_1
			set_planet_flag = starting_deposit
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = carbon_world
				days = -1
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = antirumgon_codex
				days = -1
			}
			create_pirate_country = yes
			event_target:pirate_country = {
				create_leader = {
					class = admiral
					species = event_target:batarianSpecies
					name = "Red Qorayk"
					skill = 1
					traits = {
						trait = random_trait
					}
				}				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_modifier = pirate_power
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = pirate_power
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				establish_communications_no_message = event_target:pirate_country
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_Pirate_Station"
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:pirate_country
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Pirate_Nest"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 6
						angle = 120
					}
				}
			}			
			create_fleet = {
				name = "Red's Raiders"
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:pirate_country
					set_fleet_flag = pirate_home_system_fleet
					while = {
						count = 1
						create_ship = {
							name = "Khi'shar"
							design = "NAME_Brigand"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 6
						create_ship = {
							name = random
							design = "NAME_Reaver"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					assign_leader = last_created_leader					
					set_fleet_flag = pirate_home_system_fleet
					set_formation_scale = 2
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
					set_aggro_range = 150
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 10
						angle = 120
					}
				}
			}			
		}			
    }
}

				create_pop = { species = event_target:turianSpecies }
			}
			while = {
				count = 1
				create_pop = { species = event_target:salarianSpecies }
			}
			set_owner = event_target:citadel_council
		}	
	}	

    init_effect = { 
		spawn_megastructure = { 
			type = "argosrho_shadowsea_massrelay" 
			name = "Argos_5_Relay"
			orbit_angle = 192 
			orbit_distance = 200
			
		} 
	}	
}

	name = "Patella"

		radius = 250
	}

	planet = {
		name = "Patella"
		class = "pc_a_star"
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = 33
		has_ring = no
		init_effect = {
			create_country = {
				name_list = btr_merc
				species = event_target:humanSpecies
				type = mercenary
				civics = { civic = civic_anarcho_tribalism }
				origin = "origin_default"
				flag = {
					icon={
						category="masseffect"
						file="Blue Suns.dds"
					}
					background={
						category="backgrounds"
						file="00_solid.dds"
					}
					colors={
						"blue"
						"grey"
						"null"
						"null"
					}
				}
				ethos = {
					ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
					ethic = ethic_xenophobe
				}
				ignore_initial_colony_error = yes
			}
			last_created_country = {
				set_graphical_culture = pirate_01
				save_global_event_target_as = blue_suns
				set_country_flag = blue_suns
				set_name = "Blue Suns"
				create_ship_design = { design = "NAME_Marauder_Starbase" }
				add_ship_design = last_created_design
			}
			create_fleet = {
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:blue_suns
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Warrior_Freehold"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 230
						angle = 40
					}				
				}
			}
			create_fleet = {
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:blue_suns
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Warrior_Freehold"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 230
